#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x26AD [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  1: 0x26AE [0x03] Work_Zone[1] = 1*
  2: 0x26B3 [0x43] SEND_EVENT_UPDATE: Send pending tag to server (packet 0x005B)
  3: 0x26B5 [0x43] SEND_EVENT_UPDATE: Check pending flag (skip if not pending)
  4: 0x26B7 [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x26BC)
  5: 0x26BA [0x21] END_EVENT
  6: 0x26BB [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

SUBROUTINE_26BC:
  7: 0x26BC [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[1] = Work_Zone[3]
```
